/*
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
------------------------------------CLUB DATA TABLE-------------------------------------
*/


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS records_clubs ;
CREATE TABLE records_clubs ( id Serial , name VARCHAR(255) , email VARCHAR(255) , mobile VARCHAR(255) , tmiclubid VARCHAR(255) , suburb VARCHAR(255) , city VARCHAR(255) , country VARCHAR(255) , president VARCHAR(255) , vpeducation VARCHAR(255) , vpmembership VARCHAR(255) , vppublicrelations VARCHAR(255) , secretary VARCHAR(255) , sergeantatarms VARCHAR(255) , treasurer VARCHAR(255) , created TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP , createdby VARCHAR(255) , updated TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP , updatedby VARCHAR(255) );

SELECT * FROM records_qualifications ;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS records_projects ;
CREATE TABLE records_projects ( id Serial , membersID bigint(40) unsigned , qualificationsID bigint(40) unsigned , projectsID bigint(40) unsigned , projectdate DATE , created TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP , createdby VARCHAR(255) , updated TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP , updatedby VARCHAR(255) );

/*==========================================================================================
ADD FORGIEGN KEYS TO TABLES
=========================================================================================*/



ALTER TABLE records_projects
	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( membersID ) REFERENCES records_members ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( projectsID ) REFERENCES tmi_projects ( id ) ; 

ALTER TABLE records_qualifications
	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( membersID ) REFERENCES records_members ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( qualificationsID ) REFERENCES tmi_qualifications ( id ) ; 

ALTER TABLE records_lastrole
	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( membersID ) REFERENCES records_members ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( rolesID ) REFERENCES tmi_roles ( id ) ; 
   	
ALTER TABLE records_lastrole
	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( membersID ) REFERENCES records_members ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( rolesID ) REFERENCES tmi_roles ( id ) ; 

ALTER TABLE data_pastagendas
	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( membersID ) REFERENCES records_members ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( projectsID ) REFERENCES tmi_projects ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( rolesID ) REFERENCES tmi_roles ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( clubsID ) REFERENCES records_clubs ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( qualificationsID ) REFERENCES tmi_qualifications ( id ) ,
   	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( manualsID ) REFERENCES tmi_manuals ( id );



ALTER TABLE records_members
	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( clubsID ) REFERENCES records_clubs ( id ) ;
	
ALTER TABLE data_tmiawards
	ADD FOREIGN KEY ( membersID ) REFERENCES records_members ( id ) ;
